  242. M G: candragopa-; This may be the Buddhist author Candragomin who is said to have authored a large number of texts, according to T─Бran─Бtha: “in all he composed four hundred and thirty-two separate works, of which … one hundred and eight were treatises on secular knowledge” including “fine arts, grammar, logic, medicine, prosody, dramaturgy, dictionary, poetics, astronomy, etc.” (trans. Chimpa & Chattopadhyaya, pp. 206-7). Possibly Medh─Бtithi is noting that he did not want to follow the example of Candragomin to be too prolix. ↩︎
